posted:Posted February 23, 2024
msg:Let me start with the conclusion: This is a hotel that combines natural landscape, pastoral joy and humanistic charm. When the weather is good, you can overlook the Golden Summit of Emei from the large panoramic balcony. The hotel covers a large area, so you will never see people following the crowd. It is the off-season, and walking around the hotel campus almost feels like a private estate, which is very suitable for relaxing. If you want to have an escapist experience away from the hustle and bustle of the world and be at ease in the natural mountains and rivers, this hotel will not let you down.

Breakfast: The hotel's all-day dining restaurant has a lot to choose from, but there is no a la carte breakfast menu. Compared with resort hotels of the same level, it scores 80 points.

Service: Tangtang's service is attentive and meticulous, and he has a good sense of proportion. He does not appear to be deliberately enthusiastic or alienated. All requests are responded to in a timely manner.

Hot springs: I thought it would be very cold to soak in hot springs outdoors during this season, but it turned out that I was overly worried. The hotel is located near mountains and rivers, and it is very quiet at night. You can only hear the gurgling water. It is very pleasant to soak in a hot spring in such an environment. However, the hot spring water has no mineral taste. According to the staff's explanation, they use mountain spring water from the surface and heat it for guests to use. Later, when the water was turned on in the morning, it was found that the water was cold, which confirmed that the hot spring water used in their home was not pumped from underneath.

msg:I didn‚Äôt plan to travel far during the Spring Festival this year, so I made a reservation in advance at the Hantian Resort Hotel at the foot of Mount Emei. The crowds were not at peak when we checked in, so housekeeper Dandan thoughtfully helped us arrange a room upgrade. The location of the room is good, you can overlook the top of Mount Emei while lying on the bed. The service staff, whether it is the front desk or the cleaning lady, are very friendly and well-trained.
       The hotel environment is very good. Whether it is walking around or taking a sightseeing car to Yepo Coffee to warm up and stay there for an afternoon with coffee and books, the experience is very good. If you want to find delicious food, you can drive for about 10 minutes to the Emei Maluqiao Food Circle nearby, which is very convenient. When the weather is fine, Mount Emei is covered in thin snow and is particularly beautiful. When you think about the spring flowers blooming or the lush greenery in the rice fields, you may consider painting this area a second time. In addition, the hotel is also very pet-friendly, a thumbs up! If you want a clean, relaxing and relaxing trip, it is worth recommending Amway!
What can be improved:
      The private hot spring pool is on the terrace. In winter, the temperature is not very high. When the water is filled, the temperature drops and it is almost impossible to take a dip. I stayed there for four days and three nights and didn't get any luck once.
      In addition, the hair dryer provided in the room is Dyson, a good brand, but the mouthpiece should not be a large flower head that is rarely used, but should be equipped with the most commonly used duckbill hair dryer.
